msg:There is a bus No. 20 from Yangzhou East to the hotel, the fare is 2 yuan, door to door! The ride takes about 40 minutes, which is very worthwhile! (You can get a Yangzhou bus card from zfb, you have to recharge before you can swipe the card, and the recharge amount is optional.)
The location is excellent. The hotel is in the city center, opposite Yechun and Fuchun, and you can walk to Dongguan Street and Wenchang Pavilion.
The room is very good, the small refrigerator is free, and the shower gel is divided into day and night use... The sanitary facilities are very new and clean. The bath water is not very big, but it is still comfortable. Alcohol disinfection cotton pads are provided.
The view outside the window is good, and there is free freshly ground coffee and various teas in the lobby~Ôøº
The exhaust fan and light in the bathroom are on the same switch. If it is turned off at night, there will be smoke backflow. The hotel front desk gave an air purifier very well, but it still doesn‚Äôt work... Just don‚Äôt turn off the exhaust switch.
The rooftop is quite magical! I booked the hotel because of the rooftop, but... it was not turned on on the first day, and the lights were not turned on on the second night. I was shocked... With such a unique rooftop, shouldn't we have afternoon tea or something?
The hotel has a lot of breakfast options, 7:00-10:00. It costs 58/person alone, and if it is included in the room rate, it is equivalent to an extra 30+, which is very worthwhile!
There are souvenirs when you check out! The service is really considerate and responsive!
